    Advanced liquidation risk management system for Bybit trading.

    This system provides: 1. Accurate liquidation price calculations for all contract types 2. Real-time risk monitoring and alerting 3. Portfolio-level risk assessment 4. Stress testing and scenario analysis 5. Dynamic position sizing with risk constraints 6. Liquidation avoidance strategies

    src.bot.data.historical_data_manager.HistoricalDataManager
